## <a name="summary"></a><span data-ttu-id="445d4-109">Summary</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="445d4-109">Summary</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="445d4-110">Azure HDInsight is one of the most popular services among enterprise customers for open-source Hadoop and Spark analytics on Azure.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="445d4-110">Azure HDInsight is one of the most popular services among enterprise customers for open-source Hadoop and Spark analytics on Azure.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="445d4-111">With the [plus 50 percent price cut on HDInsight](https://azure.microsoft.com/blog/azure-hdinsight-announcements-significant-price-reduction-and-amazing-new-capabilities/#_blank), customers moving to the cloud are reaping more savings than ever.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="445d4-111">With the [plus 50 percent price cut on HDInsight](https://azure.microsoft.com/blog/azure-hdinsight-announcements-significant-price-reduction-and-amazing-new-capabilities/#_blank), customers moving to the cloud are reaping more savings than ever.</span></span>

## <a name="new-features"></a><span data-ttu-id="445d4-112">New features</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="445d4-112">New features</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="445d4-113">The new updates and capabilities fall in to the following categories:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="445d4-113">The new updates and capabilities fall in to the following categories:</span></span>

1.  <span data-ttu-id="445d4-114">***Update Hadoop and other open-source projects*** – In addition to 1000+ bug fixes across 20+ open-source projects, this update contains a new version of **Spark (2.3)** and **Kafka (1.0)**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="445d4-114">***Update Hadoop and other open-source projects*** – In addition to 1000+ bug fixes across 20+ open-source projects, this update contains a new version of **Spark (2.3)** and **Kafka (1.0)**.</span></span>

    <span data-ttu-id="445d4-115">a.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="445d4-115">a.</span></span>  [<span data-ttu-id="445d4-116">**New features in Spark 2.3**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="445d4-116">**New features in Spark 2.3**</span></span>](https://spark.apache.org/releases/spark-release-2-3-0.html)

    <span data-ttu-id="445d4-117">b.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="445d4-117">b.</span></span>  [<span data-ttu-id="445d4-118">**New features in Kafka 1.0**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="445d4-118">**New features in Kafka 1.0**</span></span>](https://www.apache.org/dist/kafka/1.0.0/RELEASE_NOTES.html)

2.  <span data-ttu-id="445d4-119">***Update R Server 9.1 to Machine Learning Services 9.3*** – With this release, we are providing data scientists and engineers with the best of open source enhanced with algorithmic innovations and ease of operationalization, all available in their preferred language with the speed of Apache Spark.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="445d4-119">***Update R Server 9.1 to Machine Learning Services 9.3*** – With this release, we are providing data scientists and engineers with the best of open source enhanced with algorithmic innovations and ease of operationalization, all available in their preferred language with the speed of Apache Spark.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="445d4-120">This release expands upon the capabilities offered in R Server with added support for Python, leading to the cluster name change from R Server to ML Services.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="445d4-120">This release expands upon the capabilities offered in R Server with added support for Python, leading to the cluster name change from R Server to ML Services.</span></span> 

3.  <span data-ttu-id="445d4-121">***Support for Azure Data Lake Storage Gen2*** – HDInsight will support the Preview release of Azure Data Lake Storage Gen2.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="445d4-121">***Support for Azure Data Lake Storage Gen2*** – HDInsight will support the Preview release of Azure Data Lake Storage Gen2.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="445d4-122">In the available regions, customers will be able to choose an ADLS Gen2 account as the Primary or Secondary store for their HDInsight clusters.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="445d4-122">In the available regions, customers will be able to choose an ADLS Gen2 account as the Primary or Secondary store for their HDInsight clusters.</span></span>

4.  <span data-ttu-id="445d4-123">***HDInsight Enterprise Security Package Updates (Preview)*** – (Preview) [Virtual Network Service Endpoints](https://docs.microsoft.com/en-us/azure/virtual-network/virtual-network-service-endpoints-overview) support for Azure Blob Storage, ADLS Gen1, Cosmos DB, and Azure DB.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="445d4-123">***HDInsight Enterprise Security Package Updates (Preview)*** – (Preview) [Virtual Network Service Endpoints](https://docs.microsoft.com/en-us/azure/virtual-network/virtual-network-service-endpoints-overview) support for Azure Blob Storage, ADLS Gen1, Cosmos DB, and Azure DB.</span></span>

    -   <https://spark.apache.org/releases/spark-release-2-3-0.html#deprecations>

## <a name="upgrading"></a><span data-ttu-id="445d4-1775">Upgrading</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="445d4-1775">Upgrading</span></span>
